[30;1m95 | [0m[35m### Model components[0m
[30;1m96 | [0m[35m* Autoregression: Autocorrelation modelling - linear or NN (AR-Net).[0m
[30;1m97 | [0m[35m* Trend: Piecewise linear trend with optional automatic changepoint detection.[0m
[30;1m98 | [0m[35m* Seasonality: Fourier terms at different periods such as yearly, daily, weekly, hourly.[0m
[30;1m99 | [0m[35m* Lagged regressors: Lagged observations (e.g temperature sensor) - linear or NN.[0m
[30;1m100 | [0m[35m* Future regressors: In advance known features (e.g. temperature forecast) - linear or NN.[0m
[30;1m101 | [0m[35m* Events: Country holidays & recurring custom events.[0m

[30;1m134 | [0m[35m### Model components[0m
[30;1m135 | [0m[35m* Autoregression: Autocorrelation modelling - linear or NN (AR-Net).[0m
[30;1m136 | [0m[35m* Trend: Piecewise linear trend with optional automatic changepoint detection.[0m
[30;1m137 | [0m[35m* Seasonality: Fourier terms at different periods such as yearly, daily, weekly, hourly.[0m
[30;1m138 | [0m[35m* Lagged regressors: Lagged observations (e.g temperature sensor) - linear or NN.[0m
[30;1m139 | [0m[35m* Future regressors: In advance known features (e.g. temperature forecast) - linear or NN.[0m
[30;1m140 | [0m[35m* Events: Country holidays & recurring custom events.[0m
